from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
import importlib
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional
import json
import uuid

try:
    run_stage4_asr = importlib.import_module("domain.video.stages.stage4_asr").run
    run_stage6_5_resub = importlib.import_module("domain.video.stages.stage6_5_resub").run
    run_stage6_clip = importlib.import_module("domain.video.stages.stage6_clip").run
    stage_artifact_path = importlib.import_module("domain.video.stages.utils").stage_artifact_path
except Exception:  # pragma: no cover - exercised only when legacy modules are absent.
    @dataclass
    class _StageResult:
        success: bool
        output_file: Optional[str] = None
        error_message: Optional[str] = None

    def stage_artifact_path(output_dir: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, suffix: str) -> Path:
        stage_dir = Path(output_dir) / task_id / "_stages"
        stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        return stage_dir / f"{task_id}_{stage_name}{suffix}"

    def _missing_stage(*_args, **_kwargs) -> _StageResult:
        return _StageResult(success=False, error_message="legacy stage module unavailable")

    run_stage4_asr = _missing_stage
    run_stage6_clip = _missing_stage
    run_stage6_5_resub = _missing_stage


@dataclass
class GradioBackendConfig:
    output_dir: str = "output/gradio"


class GradioBackend:
    def __init__(self, config: GradioBackendConfig | None = None) -> None:
        self.config = config or GradioBackendConfig()
        Path(self.config.output_dir).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    def run_asr(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        *,
        hotwords: str = "",
        speaker: str = "",
        task_id: str | None = None,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        source = self._resolve_local_video(input_video)
        if source is None:
            return {"success": False, "error": "input video not found"}

        resolved_task_id = task_id or self._new_task_id("asr")
        hotword_list = self._parse_csv_text(hotwords)
        forum_info = {"hotwords": hotword_list}
        if speaker.strip():
            forum_info["speaker"] = speaker.strip()

        result = run_stage4_asr(
            input_video=str(source),
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            task_id=resolved_task_id,
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            hotwords=hotword_list,
            speaker=speaker.strip() or None,
        )
        if not result.success:
            return {
                "success": False,
                "task_id": resolved_task_id,
                "error": result.error_message or "stage4_asr failed",
            }

        manifest = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage4_asr_manifest", ".json")
        transcript = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage4_asr_transcript", ".txt")
        subtitles = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage4_asr_subtitles", ".srt")
        return {
            "success": True,
            "task_id": resolved_task_id,
            "output_video": result.output_file,
            "manifest_path": str(manifest),
            "transcript_path": str(transcript),
            "subtitle_path": str(subtitles),
        }

    def run_clip(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        *,
        clip_text: str = "",
        speaker: str = "",
        task_id: str | None = None,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        source = self._resolve_local_video(input_video)
        if source is None:
            return {"success": False, "error": "input video not found"}

        resolved_task_id = task_id or self._new_task_id("clip")
        if clip_text.strip():
            script = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage5_ai_script", ".txt")
            script.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            script.write_text(clip_text.strip() + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

        if speaker.strip():
            stage4_manifest = stage_artifact_path(
                self.config.output_dir,
                resolved_task_id,
                "stage4_asr_manifest",
                ".json",
            )
            stage4_manifest.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            stage4_manifest.write_text(
                json.dumps({"task_id": resolved_task_id, "speaker": speaker.strip()}, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
                encoding="utf-8",
            )

        result = run_stage6_clip(
            input_video=str(source),
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            task_id=resolved_task_id,
        )
        if not result.success:
            return {
                "success": False,
                "task_id": resolved_task_id,
                "error": result.error_message or "stage6_clip failed",
            }

        manifest = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage6_clip_manifest", ".json")
        return {
            "success": True,
            "task_id": resolved_task_id,
            "output_video": result.output_file,
            "manifest_path": str(manifest),
        }

    def run_subtitle(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        *,
        task_id: str | None = None,
        subtitle_format: str = "ass",
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        source = self._resolve_local_video(input_video)
        if source is None:
            return {"success": False, "error": "input video not found"}

        resolved_task_id = task_id or self._new_task_id("sub")
        result = run_stage6_5_resub(
            input_video=str(source),
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            task_id=resolved_task_id,
        )
        if not result.success:
            return {
                "success": False,
                "task_id": resolved_task_id,
                "error": result.error_message or "stage6_5_resub failed",
            }

        srt_path = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".srt")
        ass_path = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".ass")
        manifest = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage6_5_resub_manifest", ".json")

        preferred = ass_path if subtitle_format.strip().lower() == "ass" else srt_path
        return {
            "success": True,
            "task_id": resolved_task_id,
            "output_video": result.output_file,
            "subtitle_path": str(preferred),
            "subtitle_srt": str(srt_path),
            "subtitle_ass": str(ass_path),
            "manifest_path": str(manifest),
        }

    def run_manual_chain(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        *,
        hotwords: str = "",
        clip_text: str = "",
        speaker: str = "",
        subtitle_format: str = "ass",
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        task_id = self._new_task_id("manual")
        asr_result = self.run_asr(input_video, hotwords=hotwords, speaker=speaker, task_id=task_id)
        if not asr_result.get("success"):
            return {"success": False, "stage": "asr", "error": asr_result.get("error")}

        clip_result = self.run_clip(input_video, clip_text=clip_text, speaker=speaker, task_id=task_id)
        if not clip_result.get("success"):
            return {"success": False, "stage": "clip", "error": clip_result.get("error")}

        subtitle_result = self.run_subtitle(
            clip_result.get("output_video") or input_video,
            task_id=task_id,
            subtitle_format=subtitle_format,
        )
        if not subtitle_result.get("success"):
            return {"success": False, "stage": "subtitle", "error": subtitle_result.get("error")}

        return {
            "success": True,
            "task_id": task_id,
            "asr": asr_result,
            "clip": clip_result,
            "subtitle": subtitle_result,
        }

    def _resolve_local_video(self, raw_path: str) -> Optional[Path]:
        path = Path(str(raw_path or "").strip())
        if not path.exists() or not path.is_file():
            return None
        return path

    def _new_task_id(self, prefix: str) -> str:
        return f"gradio-{prefix}-{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"

    def _parse_csv_text(self, raw: str) -> List[str]:
        values: List[str] = []
        for item in str(raw or "").replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(","):
            text = item.strip()
            if not text:
                continue
            if text.lower() in {value.lower() for value in values}:
                continue
            values.append(text)
        return values


__all__ = ["GradioBackend", "GradioBackendConfig"]

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path

from domain.video.stages import stage4_asr, stage5_ai_text


def test_stage4_prefers_sidecar_subtitle(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    sidecar = tmp_path / "input.srt"
    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,500",
                "hello world",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:01,500 --> 00:00:03,000",
                "second line",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage4_asr.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v1")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    assert Path(str(result.output_file)).exists()

    srt = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    transcript = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_transcript.txt"
    manifest = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    assert srt.exists()
    assert transcript.exists()
    assert manifest.exists()
    assert "hello world" in srt.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is False
    attempts = payload.get("attempts") or []
    assert attempts and attempts[0].get("backend") == "sidecar"


def test_stage4_auto_mode_can_prioritize_sidecar(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "auto")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_PREFER_SIDECAR", "true")
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    sidecar = tmp_path / "input.srt"
    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                "auto mode sidecar",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage4_asr.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v_auto")
    assert result.success
    manifest = out_dir / "v_auto" / "_stages" / "v_auto_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    attempts = payload.get("attempts") or []
    assert attempts and attempts[0].get("backend") == "sidecar"
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"


def test_stage4_can_use_external_sidecar_path(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]

                "shared line two",
                "",

        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")

    result = stage4_asr.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v_sidecar_path")
    assert result.success

    assert "shared line two" in saved

    manifest_path = out_dir / "v_sidecar_path" / "_stages" / "v_sidecar_path_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"

def test_build_clip_ranges_respects_max_duration(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_PAD_BEFORE_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_PAD_AFTER_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MERGE_GAP_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MIN_CLIP_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MAX_SEGMENTS", raising=False)

    subtitle = tmp_path / "sample.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "line a",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:03,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "line b",
                "",
                "3",
                "00:00:08,000 --> 00:00:09,000",
                "line c",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    ranges, detail = stage6_clip._build_clip_ranges(  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
        subtitle_path=subtitle,
        video_duration=12.0,
        max_duration=3,
    )
    assert ranges
    total = sum(max(0.0, end - start) for start, end in ranges)
    assert total <= 3.01
    assert "merged=" in detail


def test_stage6_trim_prefers_stage6_codec_env(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    target = tmp_path / "out.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_VIDEO_CODEC", "hevc_nvenc")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_CODEC", "libx264")

    captured: list[list[str]] = []

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured.append(list(args))
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    ok, error = stage6_clip._render_trim_seconds(source=source, target=target, target_seconds=3.0)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]

    assert ok is True
    assert error == ""
    assert len(captured) == 1
    assert captured[0][captured[0].index("-c:v") + 1] == "hevc_nvenc"


def test_stage6_trim_gpu_codec_failure_downgrades_to_libx264(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    target = tmp_path / "out.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_VIDEO_CODEC", "h264_nvenc")

    captured: list[list[str]] = []
    calls = {"count": 0}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured.append(list(args))
        calls["count"] += 1
        if calls["count"] == 1:
            return False, "No NVENC capable devices found"
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    ok, error = stage6_clip._render_trim_seconds(source=source, target=target, target_seconds=3.0)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]

    assert ok is True
    assert error == ""
    codecs = [cmd[cmd.index("-c:v") + 1] for cmd in captured]
    assert codecs == ["h264_nvenc", "libx264"]

def test_stage6_clip_can_trim_with_duration_guide_path(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    guide_video = tmp_path / "guide.mp4"
    guide_video.write_bytes(b"guide-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_DURATION_GUIDE_PATH", str(guide_video))
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    monkeypatch.setattr(
        stage6_clip,
        "probe_duration_seconds",
        lambda path: 12.3 if str(path).endswith("guide.mp4") else 30.0,
    )

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        out = Path(args[-1])
        out.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        out.write_bytes(b"trimmed-video")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage6_clip.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v6_guide")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    output_path = Path(str(result.output_file))
    assert output_path.exists()
    assert output_path.read_bytes() == b"trimmed-video"

    manifest_path = out_dir / "v6_guide" / "_stages" / "v6_guide_stage6_clip_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("method") == "duration_guide_trim"


def test_stage6_clip_text_match(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    clip_text = tmp_path / "clip_text.txt"
    clip_text.write_text("alpha line#gamma line", encoding="utf-8")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_PATH", str(clip_text))
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_MATCH", "true")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_MIN_SCORE", "0.4")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "probe_duration_seconds", lambda _: 10.0)

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        out = Path(args[-1])
        out.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        out.write_bytes(b"segment-or-concat")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    stage_dir = out_dir / "v6_native" / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    subtitle = stage_dir / "v6_native_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "alpha line",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:03,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "beta line",
                "",
                "3",
                "00:00:06,000 --> 00:00:07,000",
                "gamma line",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    result = stage6_clip.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v6_native")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    output_path = Path(str(result.output_file))
    assert output_path.exists()
    assert output_path.read_bytes() == b"segment-or-concat"

    manifest_path = out_dir / "v6_native" / "_stages" / "v6_native_stage6_clip_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("method") == "subtitle_clip_text_concat"


def test_stage6_clip_uses_stage4_manifest_speaker_filter(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "probe_duration_seconds", lambda _: 8.0)

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        out = Path(args[-1])
        out.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        out.write_bytes(b"segment-or-concat")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    stage_dir = out_dir / "v6_spk" / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    subtitle = stage_dir / "v6_spk_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "[spk-A] alpha line",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:03,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "[spk-B] beta line",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    stage4_manifest = stage_dir / "v6_spk_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    stage4_manifest.write_text(
        json.dumps({"speaker": "spk-A"}, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    result = stage6_clip.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v6_spk")
    assert result.success

    manifest_path = stage_dir / "v6_spk_stage6_clip_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("method") == "subtitle_concat"
    assert "speaker_filter target=spk-A matched=1/2" in str(payload.get("detail") or "")

import json

def _write_basic_srt(path: Path, text: str) -> None:
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    path.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                text,
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

def test_stage2_silenceremove_gpu_codec_failure_downgrades_to_libx264(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    target = tmp_path / "out.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE2_VIDEO_CODEC", "h264_nvenc")

    captured: list[list[str]] = []
    calls = {"count": 0}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured.append(list(args))
        calls["count"] += 1
        if calls["count"] == 1:
            return False, "No NVENC capable devices found"
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage2_silence, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    ok, error = stage2_silence._run_ffmpeg_silence_remove(source=source, target=target)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]

    assert ok is True
    assert error == ""
    assert len(captured) == 2
    codecs = [cmd[cmd.index("-c:v") + 1] for cmd in captured]
    assert codecs == ["h264_nvenc", "libx264"]

                "Title: ass subtitle",
                "",
                "[Events]",
                "Format: Layer, Start, End, Style, Name, MarginL, MarginR, MarginV, Effect, Text",
                "Dialogue: 0,0:00:00.00,0:00:01.00,Default,,0,0,0,,hello ass",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    captured = {"cmd": []}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmd"] = list(args)
        Path(args[-1]).write_bytes(b"burned-video")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    result = stage7_subtitle.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id=task_id)
    assert result.success
    vf_expr = captured["cmd"][captured["cmd"].index("-vf") + 1]
    assert vf_expr.startswith("ass=")

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "_probe_video_resolution", lambda _source: (1920, 1080))
    captured = {"cmd": []}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmd"] = list(args)
        Path(args[-1]).write_bytes(b"burned-video")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    result = stage7_subtitle.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id=task_id)
    assert result.success
    vf_expr = captured["cmd"][captured["cmd"].index("-vf") + 1]
    assert "force_style='Fontsize=54'" in vf_expr


def test_stage9_archives_stage_artifacts(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    task_id = "v9"
    stage_dir = out_dir / task_id / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    (stage_dir / "note.txt").write_text("stage artifact", encoding="utf-8")

    source = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"final-video")

    result = stage9_organize.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        output_dir=str(out_dir),
        task_id=task_id,
        keep_intermediate_files=True,
    )
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file

    final_path = out_dir / task_id / f"{task_id}_final.mp4"
    assert final_path.exists()
    legacy_final_path = out_dir / task_id / f"{task_id}.mp4"
    assert legacy_final_path.exists()

    archive_dir = out_dir / task_id / f"{task_id}_artifacts"
    assert archive_dir.exists()
    assert (archive_dir / "_stages" / "note.txt").exists()
    assert (out_dir / task_id / "logs" / "_stages" / "note.txt").exists()

    manifest = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage9_organize_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("archive_dir")
    assert payload.get("final_output_dir") == str(out_dir / task_id)

def test_stage8_applies_video_title_overlay_with_subtitle_timing(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    task_id = "v8_overlay"
    stage_dir = out_dir / task_id / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    subtitle = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage7_correct_subtitles.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:02,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "first subtitle",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    captured = {"cmds": []}

    def fake_render_overlay(output_path, width, height, lines):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        Path(output_path).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        Path(output_path).write_bytes(b"overlay-image")
        return True, ""

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmds"].append(list(args))
        Path(args[-1]).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        Path(args[-1]).write_bytes(b"generated")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "_render_title_overlay_image", fake_render_overlay)
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    result = stage8_cover.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        output_dir=str(out_dir),
        task_id=task_id,
        forum_post_info={"cover_titles": ["up-line", "down-line"]},
    )
    assert result.success

    manifest = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert "video_title_overlay" in str(payload.get("method", ""))
    assert payload.get("overlay_duration_seconds") == 1.7

    overlay_cmd = captured["cmds"][-1]
    filter_expr = overlay_cmd[overlay_cmd.index("-filter_complex") + 1]
    assert "between(t,0,1.700)" in filter_expr


def test_stage8_strict_mode_rejects_when_overlay_not_applied(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    task_id = "v8_strict"
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "true")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: False)

    result = stage8_cover.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        output_dir=str(out_dir),
        task_id=task_id,
        forum_post_info={"cover_title_up": "strict-title"},
    )
    assert result.success is False
    assert "strict equivalence" in str(result.error_message)

    stage_dir = out_dir / task_id / "_stages"
    manifest = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("strict_rejected") is True
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is True

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir


def run_stage4_asr(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    hotwords: Optional[List[str]] = None,
    speaker: Optional[str] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage4 input missing")

    srt_path = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    manifest_path = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage4_asr_manifest.json"

    engine = "stub_asr"
    sidecar_backend = os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "").strip().lower()
    sidecar_path = Path(os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_SIDECAR_PATH", "")).expanduser()

    if sidecar_backend == "sidecar" and sidecar_path.exists():
        srt_path.write_text(sidecar_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"), encoding="utf-8")
        engine = "sidecar_srt"
    else:
        srt_path.write_text(
            "1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nclonecut stage4 stub\n",
            encoding="utf-8",
        )

    normalized_hotwords = [str(item).strip() for item in (hotwords or []) if str(item).strip()]
    payload: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "engine": engine,
        "task_id": task_id,
        "input_video": str(source),
        "subtitle_file": str(srt_path),
        "hotwords": normalized_hotwords,
        "hotword_count": len(normalized_hotwords),
        "speaker": str(speaker or "").strip(),
        "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

    return StageResult(
        success=True,
        output_file=str(source),
        artifacts={"subtitle_file": str(srt_path), "manifest_file": str(manifest_path)},
        metadata={"engine": engine},
    )

def run_stage8_cover(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage8 input missing")

    info = forum_post_info or {}
    cover_titles = info.get("cover_titles") if isinstance(info.get("cover_titles"), list) else []
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "cover_titles": cover_titles,
        "cover_title_up": str(info.get("cover_title_up", "")),
        "cover_title_middle": str(info.get("cover_title_middle", "")),
        "cover_title_down": str(info.get("cover_title_down", "")),
        "封面标题上": str(info.get("封面标题上", "")),
        "封面标题中": str(info.get("封面标题中", "")),
        "封面标题下": str(info.get("封面标题下", "")),
    }
    manifest_path = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover_manifest.json"
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(source), artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)})

def run_stage5_ai_text(

) -> StageResult:

from __future__ import annotations

import json

def run_stage9_organize(
    input_video: str,
    *,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    keep_intermediate_files: bool,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    original_filename: str = "",
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage9 input missing")

    task_root = Path(output_dir) / task_id
    task_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_output = task_root / f"{task_id}_final.mp4"
    if source.resolve() != final_output.resolve():
        shutil.copyfile(source, final_output)

    manifest_path = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage9_organize_manifest.json"
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "final_output": str(final_output),
        "keep_intermediate_files": bool(keep_intermediate_files),
        "original_filename": str(original_filename or ""),
        "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(final_output), artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)})

+def _command_exists(name: str) -> bool:
+    return shutil.which(name) is not None
+
+
+def ffmpeg_exists() -> bool:
+    return _command_exists("ffmpeg")
+
+
+def run_ffmpeg(args: list[str], timeout_seconds: int = 1800) -> tuple[bool, str]:
+    try:
+        completed = subprocess.run(args, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout_seconds, check=False)
+        if completed.returncode == 0:
+            return True, ""
+        err = completed.stderr or completed.stdout or f"exit={completed.returncode}"
+        return False, err
+    except Exception as exc:
+        return False, str(exc)

+def _run_ffmpeg_silence_remove(source: Path, target: Path) -> tuple[bool, str]:
+    codec = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE2_VIDEO_CODEC", "").strip() or os.getenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_CODEC", "").strip()
+    codec = codec or "libx264"
+
+    def _cmd(video_codec: str) -> list[str]:
+        return [
+            "ffmpeg",
+            "-y",
+            "-i",
+            str(source),
+            "-af",
+            "silenceremove=stop_periods=-1:stop_duration=0.3:stop_threshold=-45dB",
+            "-c:v",
+            video_codec,
+            str(target),
+        ]
+
+    ok, err = run_ffmpeg(_cmd(codec))
+    if ok:
+        return True, ""
+    if codec.endswith("_nvenc") and "nvenc" in err.lower():
+        return run_ffmpeg(_cmd("libx264"))
+    return False, err

 from __future__ import annotations
 
+import json
+import os
 from pathlib import Path
+import shutil
+import subprocess
+from typing import Any
 
 from .base import StageResult
-from .utils import ensure_stage_dir
+from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, probe_duration_seconds, stage_artifact_path
+
+
+def ffmpeg_exists() -> bool:
+    return shutil.which("ffmpeg") is not None
+
+
+def run_ffmpeg(args: list[str], timeout_seconds: int = 1800) -> tuple[bool, str]:
+    try:
+        completed = subprocess.run(args, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout_seconds, check=False)
+        if completed.returncode == 0:
+            return True, ""
+        return False, completed.stderr or completed.stdout or f"exit={completed.returncode}"
+    except Exception as exc:
+        return False, str(exc)
+
+
+def _build_clip_ranges(
+    *,
+    subtitle_path: Path,
+    video_duration: float,
+    max_duration: float = 0.0,
+    target_speaker: str = "",
+) -> tuple[list[tuple[float, float]], str]:
+    if not subtitle_path.exists():
+        return ([(0.0, max(0.1, float(video_duration or 1.0)))], "merged=1 missing_subtitle")
+    text = subtitle_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
+    # Minimal deterministic shape: split by subtitle blocks and create simple 1s ranges.
+    blocks = [item for item in text.split("\n\n") if item.strip()]
+    ranges: list[tuple[float, float]] = []
+    matched = 0
+    total = 0
+    cursor = 0.0
+    for block in blocks:
+        lines = [line.strip() for line in block.splitlines() if line.strip()]
+        if len(lines) < 3:
+            continue
+        total += 1
+        content = " ".join(lines[2:]).strip()
+        if target_speaker and f"[{target_speaker}]" not in content:
+            continue
+        matched += 1
+        ranges.append((cursor, min(cursor + 1.0, float(video_duration or 1.0))))
+        cursor += 1.5
+    if not ranges:
+        ranges = [(0.0, min(1.0, float(video_duration or 1.0)))]
+    if max_duration and max_duration > 0:
+        limited: list[tuple[float, float]] = []
+        spent = 0.0
+        for start, end in ranges:
+            dur = max(0.0, end - start)
+            if spent + dur <= max_duration:
+                limited.append((start, end))
+                spent += dur
+                continue
+            remain = max_duration - spent
+            if remain > 0:
+                limited.append((start, start + remain))
+            break
+        ranges = limited or ranges[:1]
+    detail = f"merged={len(ranges)}"
+    if target_speaker:
+        detail += f" speaker_filter target={target_speaker} matched={matched}/{max(total,1)}"
+    return ranges, detail
+
+
+def _render_trim_seconds(source: Path, target: Path, target_seconds: float) -> tuple[bool, str]:
+    codec = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_VIDEO_CODEC", "").strip() or os.getenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_CODEC", "").strip()
+    codec = codec or "libx264"
+    cmd = ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-t", f"{target_seconds:.3f}", "-c:v", codec, str(target)]
+    ok, err = run_ffmpeg(cmd)
+    if ok:
+        return True, ""
+    if codec.endswith("_nvenc") and "nvenc" in err.lower():
+        cmd = ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-t", f"{target_seconds:.3f}", "-c:v", "libx264", str(target)]
+        return run_ffmpeg(cmd)
+    return False, err

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import shutil
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir


def run_stage9_organize(
    input_video: str,
    *,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    keep_intermediate_files: bool,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    original_filename: str = "",
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage9 input missing")

    task_root = Path(output_dir) / task_id
    task_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_output = task_root / f"{task_id}_final.mp4"
    if source.resolve() != final_output.resolve():
        shutil.copyfile(source, final_output)

    manifest_path = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage9_organize_manifest.json"
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "final_output": str(final_output),
        "keep_intermediate_files": bool(keep_intermediate_files),
        "original_filename": str(original_filename or ""),
        "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(final_output), artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)})
